***pook.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pook.html>pook</a> (20015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">poke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pook.html>poken</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:pook.html>poken</a></i> (both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*puk-</i>), which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably imitative.  See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">poke</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***poot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a> (6174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pôte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">limb, claw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, further etymology unclear. The only known Germanic cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>pote</a></i>. Outside Germanic, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>pote</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca">pota</i> may be related.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pootje.html>pootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>limb (arm or <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>) of an animal (sometimes human)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spinnen.html>Spinnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:spiders.html>Spiders</a> have eight <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> or foot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>Geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Not having a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></b> to stand on.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijf.html>Blijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Keep your <b>hands</b> off <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> of an object, e.g. furniture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruk.html>kruk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A stool with three <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Although using <i><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></i> to denote limbs of humans in normally considered rude, there are some exceptions in case of idioms like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterste.html>achterste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a>.</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">To get up on one's hind <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ruigpoot</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pootje.html>pootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> homosexual <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a> (80308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">popler</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">poplier</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">peuplier</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pōpulus</i>, with a <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> added.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">poplars</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various deciduous trees of the genus <i>Populus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Wood from the <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a> tree.</li></ol>
</body>

***populatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatie</a> (22450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populātiō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to populate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">populus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a people, population</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populaties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A population, notably used in:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quantified presence of organisms on a territory</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">statistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any mass from which a sample can be drawn</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bevolking.html>bevolking</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:populatie.html>populatie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:bevolking.html>bevolking</a>.</li>

***populier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:populier.html>populier</a> (67982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">popelier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">poplier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pōpulus</i>. The spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> adapted to the Latin in the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populier.html>populier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populier.html>populieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:populier.html>populiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:poplar.html>poplar</a>, tree of the genus <i>Populus</i>.</li></ol>

***porter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a> (6523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">portere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:portier.html>portier</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">portour</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">porteor</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">portātor</i>, from past participle of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">portāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porters.html>porters</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> luggage and related <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>.
<dl><dd><i>By the time I reached the train station I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> exhausted, but fortunately there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></b> waiting.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ant having the specialized role of carrying.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who ports software (<a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> it usable on another platform).</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">portere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">portare</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">portour</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:portier.html>portier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">portarius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gatekeeper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">porta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porters.html>porters</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person in control of the entrance to a building.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">bowling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An employee who clears and cleans tables and puts bowling <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a> away.</li>
<li>A strong, dark <a href = vnd.unilang:ale.html>ale</a>, originally favored by <a href = vnd.unilang:porters.html>porters</a>, similar to a <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a> but less strong.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>Stout</a> (malt brew).</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:porters.html>porters</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">portering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">portered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To serve as a <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a>; to carry.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:portier.html>portier</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:portier.html>portier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">portārius</i>.
</p>

***poseur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:poseur.html>poseur</a> (101112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:poseur.html>poseur</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:poseur.html>poseur</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:poseurs.html>poseurs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who affects some behaviour, style, attitude or other condition, often to impress or influence others.
<dl><dd><i>He pretends draping <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:miles.html>miles</a> of cloth <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> art, and that he’s an artist, but it’s always the same gimmick with different <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>, and he’s just a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poseur.html>poseur</a></b>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>She only dresses like that because she thinks she <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> getting the boys' attention; she doesn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> like the <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a>. She’s such a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:poseur.html>poseur</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">poser</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:positie.html>positie</a> (1217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">position</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">positiō</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>position, posture</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> position</li>

<li>the state of pregnancy</li></ol>
